<user_id>113465585542666621370< /user_id><name>Michael Wessel<//name><date>1519266558810<//date><rate>4<//rate>< text>
The main thing on the menu are Cemitas. The name refers to both the sandwich as well as the bread itself. Made from eggs and covered with sesame seeds it resembles brioche, a kind of flatbread. The stuff inside is traditionally made up of sliced avocados, meat, white cheese, onions, the herb p√°palo and a sauce.

These sandwiches are amazing. I mean, you think you know what you're going to get from that description I gave before...'everything from a taco, but on bread'...and then it's so much more. The combo of Carnitas, the fresh onion, some unknown chipotle flavored sauce, that bun with insides toasted with butter, all sitting on a bed of shredded Mexican cheese...washed down with ice cold real Coke, talk about a great lunch.

A nice little unassuming restaurant
It's a chill place to sit and have a conversation while enjoying some really tasty food. There's a good selection of sodas...Coke, Fanta, Mandarin...the good stuff. It's also really affordable. For 2 sandwiches and 2 drinks it only set us back $20. There were more expensive and less expensive dishes on the menu, but you'd have to work hard to go broke before you were stuffed. Just one sandwich had me sitting back with a satisfied smile.<//text>

< review>
I'd literally go out of my way to eat here, that's how good they are. I haven't had any bad luck here or experience. Maybe one but it was insignificant so won't really count it. The cemas are fkn good. 10/10 for me. They are good size and the huitlacoche ( corn smut, corn truffle) quesadilla is always great because is hand made tortilla. I most of the time get cueritos or milanesa and the consistency hasn't disappoint. They accept both cards and cash so that's convenient but they do charge for using card. They menu is a good size so you got a good amount of options. The men's restroom is inside the kitchen just so you know. Will keep coming and if  anything were to happen, I won't hesitate to update.</review>

<Rating>5<//Rating>< Text>
This is my favorite place for comfort food and/or my cheat meal. I always get a california burrito either human size or monster (those are the only options). But hot damn it is amazing, the monster burrito is about the size of my forearm and is simply fantastic after a long week. This place also has super great platters and tacos. You can order pretty much anything off the menu and not go wrong. I highly reccomend this place to anyone who wants some delicious late night Mexican food. Also a bonus is they stay open till around midnight usually and are on ubereats. Overall a fantastic place to spend 8-15$ on food.< /Text>

< Review>
This place is a good step above a typical fast food Mexican place. The nice thing about this location in particular is that it does have a drive thru and it's open 24 hours Thursday thru Saturday. They cook to order so don't expect the food to come out fast. The food is decent, but some of the cheese doesn't taste real and has a strange flavor to it. Also, there have been times where the guacamole tasted as if a jar of salt accidentally fell into the bowl. The service is ok. Still it's a great option for late night eats and one of the few in the area.< /Review>

<Rate>5</Rate>< text>
Menchie's has a self-service system where you pay based on how much you serve yourself. The selections are wide, basic nutritional information is posted next to the flavors, there are various a sugar-free and low calorie options, and extensive information on ingredients and more details are available on request.

The shop is clean and bright with plenty of seating. The staff is very helpful and friendly, clearly management is hands on. I'm going to be a regular.</text>

< Name>
Lisa Crowell< /Name>
< Text>
I was lucky enough to be at Folded Hills this past weekend for opening day of their new Homestead Winery and Tasting Room. OMG what a cool place this is!! They took the original farmers house - where they used to make pre prohibition wine btw - and completely renovated it while somehow still letting the history of the place shine through. Wow! This place is seriously gorgeous. I had already been to their Montecito Tasting Room (also awesome) so I knew I loved all of the wines, but this place really blew me away. We meant to pop in for an hour or so, and ended up staying all day! Bring a picnic lunch...you won't want to leave. Lots of great areas to hang, inside and out, and enjoy a wine tasting...or in our case a few bottles...of their award winning Lilly Ros√© and my favorite, August White! They also have backgammon...bocce ball...cornhole...and even yard farkle!! I'm in heaven. Whoever designed this place is a genius. Grab some bottles to go and don't forget a trucker hat! I've gotten asked like ten times already where I got it! I'll be back soon, I loved it all so much I joined the wine club! Can't wait for the private wine club party this fall!! I never used this service-- I never even knew how to while I had this account.
